=== September 12th.md ===
# September 12th

Sat on the plane to Porto. Quite ambivalent about coming back to Brazil - could easily have stayed in the UK for longer. But this way you can give the project a push  with more melodica and recorder students and some personal contacts, you can travel in Brazil, and then you can do the UK again at Christmas. Was great seeing Charlotte and Rob - had a nice Indian take-away and watched the Brass for Africa film with them last night. Did spend the whole time worrying about giving everyone COVID though. Will breath a big sigh of relief in a weeks’ time assuming everyone is still okay.

Thursday morning it was great to see Jim Trott but really embarrassed about turning up empty-handed. Bottle of wine would have covered it. Anyway, the actual conversation went well and also met his wife, Pam, and daughter Gracie. Talked about him possibly letting us use his cargo allowance, lots of good advice about fundraising and bringing students over to the UK. Also the possibility of making a video together, and I tried to steer us away from doing a tune that’s too “colonial” without offending Jim.

Jim also gave me the link and password to the Brass for Africa doc. He watched gringo favela with family the same day but we only watched theirs yesterday, not ideal. Was a very nice doc and Jim really didn’t get featured much, to his credit - unlike in Favela Brass videos, which are often very centered on you. The project was impressive but I still get the impression they don’t really have the kind of solid network of local bands that their materials imply, and I’m not 100% that all of the musicians that came to the UK came through their project. Call me cynical but there’s still something not quite adding up.

The question that I am thinking about now is: if someone were to make a film about the next year or two at Favela Brass, what would be the story? It starts with COVID hitting and the kids playing at home, then there’s some spark because of COVID and going online, which throws sets us on a quest which gets sorted in 2022.

COVID sparks:
Making videos with other groups
Talking to other band directors

Quests:
Why can’t kids have their carnival to look forward to every year?
Make a world bloco in Brazil
A world youth street music carnival, (that then goes to other countries?)

What about... a joint video with kids in street music projects to kick things off?

Who could be in it?

In London and been a bit rubbish about writing the diary. Saw Ed and Dan for a curry on Tuesday which was great - restaurant was doing a two for one offer as well. Bonus. Dan has 2 kids and Ed 3 and sounds like they have mixed feelings about the whole thing. You could be in a much worse predicament. Should have kept contact better - especially with Ed. Got a lift back with Ed and regretted it - even though COVID is much less prevalent at the mo you should have walked for your Dad’s sake.

Yesterday met Dennis Macdonagh for lunch which turned in to just drinking outside a pub near convent garden. Very glad to have this one beer rule. He’s the same old Dennis and very keen to make amends with the DYJO lot and John Ellis. Same wandering but entertaining conversation as ever. Another friend that you could have reached out to a lot sooner.

Great to catch up and talk about British school stuff and his job as head of music at St. Paul’s school and the incredibly elite students that he is teaching there. Went for pizza and then Rich Fletcher came down a bit later. Rich has got a girlfriend now which is brilliant and is getting into coding as well so interesting to chat to him about that. Uber back with face mask and window open didn’t feel too risky.

Been staying in the Penn club which is very nice - lovely breakfast with berries, yoghurt and muesli. Coffee with Shaleena this morning at pret a manger on highbury corner. She’s pretty much better from the disease that she had but has hurt her back recently. Now working on homicide and had a fairly grisly tale to tell about the current case that she was about to attend court for. Offered to take the kids to 10

Which reminds me that I didn’t write about
going to Birmingham Symphony Hall to see Chris Procter on Monday. Have to commit to this 2022 if it’s actually going to happen and it will take a lot of time effort. 

Been thinking about the Carola thing (for a change) and strongly feel that she has to go. Asked her to put Stuart MacDonald’s donated French Horn on Ebay which may turn out to be a mistake. Went to Stu Macdonald’s after and he donated 2 trombones and a load of accessories to the project. He also said that he’s quitting the shop and quite happy just to be rid of his stock. We are massively behind with our Favela Brass meetings. Angelo needs to understand that as president he needs to see that the monthly meetings happen with or without him, and that things like the meeting with the accountant move forward with or without him. We have a vice-president exactly for if he has emergencies etc.

Also youth Projects in Rio:
Rocinha
Afro-Reggae

Ok so had a coffee in Porto airport and thought of a name: “Youth Brass United”? Could work if it’s an open social media account where everyone can post what they are up to. Could also do a wix to share resources - map of projects, charts, links to individual projects, social media accounts.

About:

“Youth Brass United is an alliance of music education projects from all over the world that play funky street brass band music. We provide our students with the opportunity to rehearse and perform together - whether that be online, or as part of international exchanges, and to learn about each other’s musical cultures through the sharing of educational resources.”

September 16th

Booked the trip to Aracaju yesterday. Will it get really expensive at a time when I don’t have much income? Am I too far from the beach to enjoy it? What about the monitor situation? Will I spend the whole time worrying about the situation with Adrienne? It is irresponsible in terms of Covid? Will I get bored? Am I being unfair on Joe abandoning him again? What if Globo want to do a report on us and I have to be in Rio? How will I cope with a whole month without piano practice? Wouldn’t there have been a better option?

All of the above are reasonable concerns, but it’s good to work against your usual bias to chicken out of stuff. Go for it, make the most of it, ENJOY IT. Set yourself a nice ambitious WIG for the month and hit it for 6. Also, remember that Joe situation could get annoying again at any moment.

Told Carola that she’s down to one day a week as of next month and only working on grants now (maybe grants/applications would be the best definition). === September 17th.md ===
# September 17th

September 17th

Yesterday finished Youtube playlists and, after having a scare thinking I had lost the HD, started organizing the new Turma 1 repertoire. I think there will be a lot of medleys in there - you should be looking at building punchy 30-minute sets. This could be the project for Aracaju. You will have to write arrangements without resorting to recording, but this will be a good discipline - if orchestrators can “hear” on entire orchestra then you should be able to handle a brass band of instruments you already play.

Also made and sent video to Honk. 

Had another lovely walk up to the rock and a real moment listening to “Take it easy” by the Eagles after meditating, looking out across everything. Getting out at 3pm would be the perfect time, to catch the sunset up top. Can you get your working day finished by 3pm? In any case have to engineer as many of these walks as possible into the week - they are perfect for the afternoon lull and caffeine hangover and the thinking is really productive. As is the trumpet practice and listening to classical music on the way down (Dvorak at the mo) - struck me that classical music is from a time when people had longer attention spans, and that maybe it’s the listener that has to up their game. 

The Youth Brass United idea still seems a good one. I think it’s going to survive its week of quarantine and be worth talking to the others about.

# September 22nd, 2020

September 22nd, 2020

Had a very low-energy day yesterday - tried jacking myself up on lots of cups of tea but didn’t work. Getting back to Carola messed up morning routine let’s see if we can work that back. Confess that I may have listened to a certain song from the Wizard of Oz more than once in the last 24 hours.

Went for lunch with Mangueirinha yesterday - was fine, but reminded me that he too is one to be a little bit careful with. He said that Carola was “malandrinna”, but over the years he has also shown that he hasn’t exactly “got your back”. Keep the project moving forward and the grumblers in check.

=== September 23rd.md ===
# September 23rd

**September 23rd**

2023

You haven’t been writing diaries recently. Pretty sure that’s down to 2 things - for one, you have less time alone stewing, and the other thing is that you’re less stressed and needing to get things straight in the diary.

Summing up recent stuff:

1. You’re loving the chalet with Thamires, and moving closer and closer to living together there. Just need to check that Thamires is up for this whole thing of getting married and having kids not long after.
2. Favela Brass a million times better (for you at least!) with Pam gone. Initial signs good with Patrícia, giving more work to Carol and about to hire Iris.
3. Writing going well - solid 90 minutos each and every day working (too much coffee helps), and just need to get recording stuff now.

2020

In Aracaju and questioning it a bit. Why are you spending R$3.000 to spend a month in a house next to a main road in a city that just has one massive long beach, that you’re not even right on (30 mins walk at least to the part where you can swim) getting into a thing with a girl that you will only have to get yourself out of afterwards, and making people jealous and fuelling the idea that you have money to burn?

Good question.. The rationale was really to escape from Joe and have a nice month by the beach, a lot of fun with Adrienne, and get stuff done. That being the original mission, let’s go with that. Stop whingeing. Tell Joe the place is not suitable for 2 (which it isn’t - the road thing was actually a piece of luck). Find a way to get yourself to the beach for a run or long walk and a swim each day either first thing or in the afternoon. Have loads of sex with Adrienne and don’t overthink it, and work your ass off.

Possible timetable:

5: Up, coffee, diary, bit of trumpet

6: Down to work (WIG 1a) - 6:45 Bach Trumpet Break
7: WIG 1b - 7:45 Bach Trumpet Break
8: WIG 2a + Bach Tpt Break
9: Wig 2b + Bach Tpt
10: Whirlwind + Bach Tpt Break
11: Whirlwind + Bach Tpt Break
12: Whirlwind + Bach Tpt Break

13: Lunch + Nap

14: Beach, sex, long walks thinking things through, music
 
Been thinking a bit about Mangueirinha again. Don’t forget that he’s a bully who disrespects you in private and even in public and isn’t loyal. Don’t write him off but remember that it wasn’t just Carola…

=== September 24th, 2020.md ===
# September 24th, 2020

September 24th, 2020

Things are looking up. Went to the beach for sunset yesterday with whisky and agua de coco, just fantastic. Warm water, hardly any people and a seemingly endless stretch of beach to run up and down. Have to get in the sea every day that I possibly can here (barring rainy days, obviously). Looks like routine is going to be work till about 3pm then go to the beach. Get running in, because you are now feeling short of energy because of the lack of exercise recently.

Favela Brass admin is starting to pile up a bit - getting the accounts done in the new format ready for the meeting Friday, keeping on top of current editais, writing new Rouanet, etc. At the next meeting you should be asking to match Mangueirinha’s salary, with recent expenditures being taken into account. You have taken on Carola’s work so this really shouldn’t be too contentious.

Another thing struck me: don’t be the person who can’t get things done without going back to ask for permission for everything. Think Eisenhower - take command, present results, don’t be a baby.


=== September 26th, 2020.md ===
# September 26th, 2020

September 26th, 2020

Had a bit of a down day on Thursday, but got better after eating properly (including carangueijo and pastel de aratu) on the Orla. Adrienne is as nice a woman as you could ask for - take it easy, try not to create huge expectations and just roll with it. Have to say finding out she’s had silicone implants was a bit of a passion-killer.

Yesterday morning did things properly - out for run on the Orla at 5:30, jumped in the sea and meditated on the beach. Lovely. Came home and basically worked straight through from 8am till the meeting with the board at 8pm with breaks, desperately trying to get our accounts in order. 

Came to the meeting tired and irritable and although it went OK, we still only really scratched the surface. We haven’t had a meeting for 3 months and we need to meet much more often. Put the UK charity thing on the table but they just ummed and ahhhed about it. They were suggesting that we pay someone to write our grants, but not mention was made of the fact that I’m still not paid. Maybe best to make these points to Angelo.

Amelia finished the video and then the issue of the videos that the kids sent in via WhatsApp came up - Artu, Davi, Raissa. Amelia wants to put them in, but I just don’t think it’s worth her starting again - the quality is rubbish anyway. Anyway, you cocked up, is the bottom line.

 

=== September 27, 2020.md ===
# September 27, 2020

September 27, 2020

Bit of an off day yesterday. Falsely accused Carola of owing us one more month of salary than she actually does. Not good. Later on was a zombie for Adrienne, who kept asking you what was up (to be fair this got a bit annoying). Feeling stressed and lethargic. Pretty sure that the coffee is at the root of this (and lack of exercise, also possibly the constant road noise at home). Time to get off coffee - bought some green tea in the hope this will bring things down gently.

Also a bit stressed about cash. Spending far too much on restaurant bills at the moment - have to rein that in (having said that yesterday at Rendeiro with the guitarist was special). Wrote my job description for the board with my 9 main functions and tomorrow will let Angelo know that I want the question of my pay on the agenda. I think I basically need to just hit the basics - lots of exercise, less/no caffeine, meditation maybe even no booze, in order to get back on track.

Played pretty much all of the 28 Bach tunes in the beginner book on trumpet yesterday - to continue this and start putting them round the key would be a great Aracaju goal. 

=== September 2nd 2020.md ===
# September 2nd 2020

September 2nd 2020

Have come up with the idea of telling Carola that we’re going to re-evaluate in a months’ time. Not as drastic as firing her outright, means you will be giving her criticism direct, leaves your options open, seems fairer and also should get some decent work out of her this month. It’s a conversation that definitely requires some preparing.

Mangueirinha sent this Lei Aldir Blanc on Monday afternoon and I delayed before sending it to Carola until Tuesday morning. Not good, as the deadline was Monday 5pm in Brazil but not such an issue as the deadline has been put back. Without wanting to shift blame, why is Mangueirinha sending me this and not Carola? Same thing with another edital that someone sent me.

Had a really nice moment yesterday with the folks drinking a glass of Portuguese red wine and eating Dad’s bolognese. And another in the morning practicing Bach and sipping loose-leaf tea. Am waiting for the impending lull after being high on tea the last couple of days.
